         <div class="ff0" style="font-size:101px">
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:1151px;word-spacing:-4px;color:#416282">
           Social Networking Popular Across Globe
          </span>
         </div>
         <div class="ff13" style="font-size:86px">
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:1279px;color:#7e7e7e">
           Arab Publics Most Likely to Express Political Views Online
          </span>
         </div>
         <div class="ff7" style="font-size:79px">
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:1550px;word-spacing:-1px">
           Social networking has spread around the world
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:537px;top:1668px">
           with remarkable speed. In countries such as
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:1787px;word-spacing:-1px">
           Britain, the United States, Russia, the Czech
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:1904px;word-spacing:-1px">
           Republic and Spain, about half of all adults
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:2022px;word-spacing:-1px">
           now use Facebook and similar websites. These
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:2140px;word-spacing:-1px">
           sites are also popular in many lower-income
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:2258px;word-spacing:-1px">
           nations, where, once people have access to the
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:2376px;word-spacing:-1px">
           internet, they tend to use it for social
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:2494px">
           networking.
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:2730px;word-spacing:-1px">
           Meanwhile, cell phones have become nearly
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:2848px;word-spacing:-1px">
           ubiquitous throughout much of the world, and
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:2965px;word-spacing:-1px">
           people are using them in a variety of ways,
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:3083px;word-spacing:-2px">
           including texting and taking pictures. Smart
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:3201px;word-spacing:-1px">
           phones are also increasingly common 
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:3319px;word-spacing:-1px">
           roughly half in Britain, the U.S., and Japan
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:3437px;word-spacing:-1px">
           have one. Globally, most smart phone users
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:3555px;word-spacing:-1px">
           say they visit social networking sites on their
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:3673px;word-spacing:-1px">
           phone, while many get job, consumer, and
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:3791px;word-spacing:-2px">
           political information.
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:4027px;word-spacing:-1px">
           Technologies like these are especially popular
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:4145px;word-spacing:-1px">
           among the young and well educated. In almost
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:4263px;word-spacing:-1px">
           every country polled, people under age 30 and
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:4380px;word-spacing:-1px">
           those with a college education are more likely
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:4498px;word-spacing:-1px">
           to engage in social networking and to use a
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:4616px">
           smart phone.
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:4852px;word-spacing:-1px">
           These are among the key findings from a 21-
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:4970px;word-spacing:-1px">
           nation survey conducted by the Pew Research
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:557px;top:5088px;word-spacing:-1px">
           Centers Global Attitudes Project from March 17-April 20. The survey also finds that global
          </span>
         </div>
         <div class="ff16" style="font-size:79px">
          <span class="a" style="left:2361px;top:1648px;word-spacing:-3px;color:#416282">
           Do You Use
           <span class="w6">
           </span>
           Social Networking
          </span>
          <span class="a" style="left:2361px;top:1736px;color:#416282">
           Sites?
          </span>
         </div>

          <span class="a" style="left:2361px;top:4658px;word-spacing:-3px;color:#7e7e7e">

           <span class="l6">
            s who do
            <span class="w6">
            </span>
            not use the
            <span class="w6">
